## Section 021: Retry Backpressure Guidance

## Section 024: Scale Boundary Statement
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that the seed task-splitting bounds stand beside the entrypoint's own scale limits, the skill governs one Tauri request at a time through one packet, its modes bound the lenses applied rather than the request size, its authority ends at packet handoff where implementation and gating take over, and its dialect pair bounds platform reach, Claude-shaped and Codex-shaped consumption with anything else requiring labeled adaptation
- **supporting_reason:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because an intake skill scales by packet repetition, each request gets the same bounded treatment, and its self-limits, selective conventions, explicit exclusions of forced universality, keep packet cost flat as request volume grows
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: scope creep here means the packet swallowing implementation, design sections growing into code, or one packet spanning unrelated requests until traceability rows cross-tangle
